It opens the door to an exciting \"new classical\" chess.\r\n\r\nIn Neoclassical Chess all rules are exactly as in classical chess, except that play starts after three full moves\r\nfrom White and Black, those of a game taken at random from a large, carefully selected database of recent chess master games.\r\nAs a consequence, openings appear in proportion to their frequency in master practice, providing a single worldwide standard for play.\r\nThe app provides the initial position and the moves leading to it just before the start of play.\r\n\r\nThe app Neoclassical Chess allows chess players to play ‚ÄúNeoclassical chess‚Äù by selecting the option \"3 Nc Chess\". \r\nIt also includes Neoclassical Chess Black, the variant with the Black pieces (where the position is obtained after the third move by White, so that Blacks starts the game by choosing the third, free move) by selecting the \"2.5 Nc Chess Black\" option.
